performance estimate without leakage.\n   211→        \"\"\"\n   212→        print(\"Running walk-forward validation (single split)...\", flush=True)\n   213→\n   214→        df_sorted =        # Evaluate all individuals\n            for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n                try:\n                    print(f\"    Training individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    accuracy = (pred == y_train).mean()\n\n                    # Simple fitness based on training accuracy (we'll validate on walk-forward later)\n                    ind.fitness = accuracy\n                    print(f\"      -> fitness={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n                except Exception as e:\n     Run walk-forward validation with a single temporal split.\n        Train on data before the validation period, test on the most recent validation period.\n        This provides an honest OOS performance estimate without leakage.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Running walk-forward validation (single split)...\", flush=True)\n\n        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n\n        # Determine validation period length (e.g., 7 days)\n        val_days = ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS\n        val_rows = int(val_days * flush=True)\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        # Split: validation = most recent val_rows, training = older data\n        valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[-val_rows:].copy()\n        train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:-val_rows].copy()\n\n        # Prepare OHLC data for simulation with stop-loss\n        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n\n        # Limit training samples to most recent MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES (controls memory/time)\n        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            train_df = y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # Evolve a fresh population on the training set\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n            print(f\"  Generation {gen+1}/{ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION}\", flush=True)\n            # Evaluate individuals on training data\n            for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    # Use training accuracy as fitness for selection\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"    Training error: for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n            # Skip individuals that failed training\n            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n                print(f\"  Skipping individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} (failed training)\", flush=True)\n                continue\n            try:\n                print(f\"  Rescoring individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)}            ind.validation_metrics = v_metrics\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Validation rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n        # Get top diverse models based on validation Sharpe\n        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n\n        # Generate consensus signals on validation set\n        consensus = Define train window: [start_idx, end_idx)\n            train_end = end_idx\n            train_start = start_idx\n\n            # Define valid window: [end_idx, end_idx + valid_rows)\n            valid_start = end_idx\n            valid_end = end_idx + int(self.valid_days * 24 * 60 / 15)  # 15-min candles per day\n\n            if valid_end >= total_rows:\n                break\n\n            # Check minimum training samples\n            if train_end - train_start >= self.min_train_samples:\n                train_df = df.iloc[train_start:train_end].copy()\n                valid_df = df.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n\n                if len(valid_df) > 0:\n                    yield train_df, valid_df, valid_df.index\n\n            # Step forward\n            step_rows = int(self.step_days * 24 * 60 / 15)\n            end_idx += step_rows\n\n            # Optionally also move start forward for sliding window\n            # For expanding, start_idx stays at 0\n\n    def evaluate_folds(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        model_builder,\n        feature_fn,\n        target_col: str = \"target\",\n        time_col: str = \"open_time\"\n    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Run walk-forward evaluation.\n\n        Args:\n            df: full dataset\n            model_builder: function that returns a trained model given X_train, y_train\n            feature_fn: function to extract features from df\n            target_col: name of target column\n            time_col: name of time column\n\n        Returns:\n            dict of aggregated metrics across all folds\n        \"\"\"\n        all_metrics = []\n\n        for train_df, valid_df, test_idx in self.generate_folds(df):\n            X_train = feature_fn(train_df)\n            y_train = train_df[target_col]\n\n            X_valid = feature_fn(valid_df)\n            y_valid = valid_df[target_col]\n\n            if len(X_valid) == 0:\n                continue\n\n            # Train model\n            model = model_builder()\n            try:\n                model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n            except Exception as e:\n                continue\n\n            # Predict\n            proba = model.predict_proba(X_valid)\n            pred = model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n\n            # Metrics\n            accuracy = (pred == y_valid).mean()\n            all_metrics.append({\n                \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n                \"n_samples\": len(X_valid),\n                \"fold\": len(all_metrics)\n            })\n\n        if not all_metrics:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        # Weighted average by fold size\n        total_samples = sum(m[\"n_samples\"] for m in all_metrics)\n        weighted_accuracy = sum(m[\"accuracy\"] * m[\"n_samples\"] for m in all_metrics) / total_samples\n\n        return {\n            \"accuracy\": weighted_accuracy,\n            \"n_folds\": len(all_metrics),\n            \"total_valid_samples\": total_samples\n        }\n","numLines":142,"startLine":1,"totalLines":142}}}

At least MIN_MODELS_AGREE models must agree on direction\n    - Average confidence must exceed MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        min_models_agree: int = ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n        min_confidence: float = ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    ):\n        self.min_models_agree = min_models_agree\n        self.min_confidence = min_confidence\n\n    def decide(\n        self,\n        models: List[Individual],\n        X: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate final trading signals (UP=1, DOWN=0, NO_TRADE=-1).\n\n        Args:\n            models: list of trained model individuals\n            X: feature DataFrame to predict on\n\n        Returns:\n            Series of signals (1, 0, or -1) aligned to X.index\n        \"\"\"\n        signals = pd.Series(index=X.index, data=0)\n        probas_matrix = []\n\n        for ind in models:\n            try:\n                proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X)\n                probas_matrix.append(proba)\n            except Exception as e:\n                continue\n\n        if not probas_matrix:\n            # No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_sharpe: float = 1.0,\n        target_profit_factor: float = 1.2,\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        Prioritizes risk-adjusted returns (Sharpe) and profitability (profit factor).\n        If Sharpe or profit factor are below target, tighten thresholds to improve quality.\n        If accuracy is high but Sharpe is low, also tighten (filter out low-quality trades).\n        If bets are too low and accuracy acceptable, loosen to increase frequency.\n        \"\"\"\n        sharpe = recent_performance.get(\"sharpe\", -1000.0)\n        profit_factor = recent_performance.get(\"profit_factor\", 0.0)\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        # If we already have sufficient accuracy and activity, avoid tightening thresholds\n        # which could zero out trading. This allows the rescoring metric change to take effect.\n        if accuracy >= target_accuracy and bets_per_month >= 150:\n            # Maintain current thresholds; no adjustment this cycle\n            return\n\n        # If extremely few trades (or none), loosen to generate activity\n        if bets_per_month < 30.0:\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n            # After loosening for low activity, skip further adjustments this cycle\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n            return\n\n        # Primary: Sharpe and profitability\n        if sharpe < target_sharpe or profit_factor < target_profit_factor:\n            # Poor risk-adjusted/absolute performance: tighten to filter trades\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # Too few trades despite decent accuracy: loosen thresholds\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.02)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n        # else: keep thresholds stable\n\n        # Clamp to reasonable ranges\n        self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n        self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n\n    def get_params(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"min_models_agree\": self.min_models_agree,\n            \"min_confidence\": self.min_confidence\n        }\n","numLines":149,"startLine":1,"totalLines":149}}}

Combined transaction cost: fee + slippage\n        entry_cost = self.fee_rate + self.slippage\n        exit_cost = self.fee_rate + self.slippage\n\n        # Determine if we have high/low for stop-loss\n        use_stop = self.stop_loss_pct > 0\n        if isinstance(prices, pd.DataFrame):\n            # Expect columns: 'close', optionally 'high', 'low'\n            if 'high' in prices.columns and 'low' in prices.columns:\n                close_series = prices['close']\n                high_series = prices['high']\n                low_series = prices['low']\n            else:\n                close_series = prices['close']\n                high_series = low_series = close_series\n        else:\n            close_series = prices\n            high_series = low_series = prices\n\n        # Align signals and prices\n        signals = signals.reindex(close_series.index).fillna(-1)\n\n        # Build equity curve indexed by signals.index\n        equity = pd.Series(index=signals.index, dtype=float)\n        equity.iloc[0] = capital\n\n        # Iterate through each timestamp, use signal to open a trade that closes at next timestamp\n        for i in range(len(signals) - 1):\n            sig = signals.iloc[i]\n            current_price = close_series.iloc[i]\n            next_close = close_series.iloc[i+1]\n            next_high = high_series.iloc[i+1]\n            next_low = low_series.iloc[i+1]\n\n            if sig == -1:\n                # No trade, carry forward capital\n                equity.iloc[i+1] = capital\n                continue\n\n            # Determine entry price with cost\n            if sig == 1:  # long\n                entry = current_price * (1 + entry_cost)\n                # Determine exit price considering stop-loss\n                stop_price = entry * (1 - self.stop_loss_pct) if use_stop else None\n                exit_price = next_close * (1 - exit_cost)\n                if use_stop and next_low <= stop_price:\n                    # Stop triggered: exit at stop price (with exit cost)\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 - exit_cost)\n                ret = (exit_price / entry) - 1\n            else:  # short\n                entry = current_price * (1 - entry_cost)\n                stop_price = entry * (1 + self.stop_loss_pct) if use_stop else None\n                exit_price = next_close * (1 + exit_cost)\n                if use_stop and next_high >= stop_price:\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 + exit_cost)\n                ret = (entry / exit_price) - 1\n\n            # Apply bet size\n            capital *= (1 + ret * self.bet_size)\n\n            self.trades.append({\n                \"entry_time\": signals.index[i],\n                \"exit_time\": signals.index[i+1],\n                \"entry_price\": entry,\n                \"exit_price\": exit_price,\n                \"return\": ret,\n                \"pnl\": capital - self.initial_capital,\n                \"stopped\": use_stop and ((sig == 1 and next_low <= stop_price) or (sig == 0 and next_high >= stop_price))\n            })\n\n            equity.iloc[i+1] = capital\n\n        # Fill any remaining NaNs in equity with last value\n        equity = equity.ffill()\n\n        self.equity_curve = equity\n\n        # Calculate metrics\n        self.metrics = self._compute_metrics()\n\n        return self.metrics\n\n    def _compute_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"Compute metrics from simulation.\"\"\"\n        if not self.trades:\n            return {\n                \"accuracy\": 0.0,\n                \"bets_per_month\": 0.0,\n                \"sharpe\": 0.0,\n                \"max_drawdown\": 0.0,\n                \"total_return\": 0.0,\n                \"n_trades\": 0,\n                \"profit_factor\": 0.0,\n                \"final_equity\": self.initial_capital\n            }\n\n        returns = [t[\"return\"] for t in self.trades]\n        winning = sum(1 for r in returns if r > 0)\n        accuracy = winning / len(returns)\n\n        # Bets per month (entries)\n        n_entries = len(self.trades)\n        if self.equity_curve is not None and len(self.equity_curve) > 0:\n            period_days = len(self.equity_curve) / (24 * 4)  # 15-min candles to days\n        else:\n            period_days = 0\n        months = period_days / 30.44\n        bets_per_month = n_entries / months if months > 0 else 0\n\n        # Sharpe\n        if self.equity_curve is not None:\n            eq_returns = self.equity_curve.pct_change().dropna()\n            if eq_returns.std() > 0:\n                sharpe = (eq_returns.mean() / eq_returns.std()) * np.sqrt(365 * 24 * 4)\n            else:\n                sharpe = 0.0\n\n            # Max drawdown\n            running_max = self.equity_curve.expanding().max()\n            drawdown = (self.equity_curve - running_max) / running_max\n            max_drawdown = abs(drawdown.min())\n        else:\n            sharpe = 0.0\n            max_drawdown = 0.0\n\n        total_return = (self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] - self.initial_capital) / self.initial_capital\n\n        gross_profit = sum(r for r in returns if r > 0)\n        gross_loss = abs(sum(r for r in returns if r < 0))\n        profit_factor = gross_profit / (gross_loss + 1e-10)\n\n        return {\n            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n            \"bets_per_month\": bets_per_month,\n            \"sharpe\": sharpe,\n            \"max_drawdown\": max_drawdown,\n            \"total_return\": total_return,\n            \"n_trades\": len(self.trades),\n            \"profit_factor\": profit_factor,\n            \"final_equity\": self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] if self.equity_curve is not None else self.initial_capital,\n            \"gross_profit\": gross_profit,\n            \"gross_loss\": gross_loss\n        }\n\n    def get_equity_curve(self) -> pd.Series:\n        return self.equity_curve\n\n    def get_trades(self) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        return pd.DataFrame(self.trades)\n","numLines":204,"startLine":1,"totalLines":204}}}

Combined transaction cost: fee + slippage\n        entry_cost = self.fee_rate + self.slippage\n        exit_cost = self.fee_rate + self.slippage\n\n        # Determine if we have high/low for stop-loss\n        use_stop = self.stop_loss_pct > 0\n        if isinstance(prices, pd.DataFrame):\n            # Expect columns: 'close', optionally 'high', 'low'\n            if 'high' in prices.columns and 'low' in prices.columns:\n                close_series = prices['close']\n                high_series = prices['high']\n                low_series = prices['low']\n            else:\n                close_series = prices['close']\n                high_series = low_series = close_series\n        else:\n            close_series = prices\n            high_series = low_series = prices\n\n        # Align signals and prices\n        signals = signals.reindex(close_series.index).fillna(-1)\n\n        # Build equity curve indexed by signals.index\n        equity = pd.Series(index=signals.index, dtype=float)\n        equity.iloc[0] = capital\n\n        # Iterate through each timestamp, use signal to open a trade that closes at next timestamp\n        for i in range(len(signals) - 1):\n            sig = signals.iloc[i]\n            current_price = close_series.iloc[i]\n            next_close = close_series.iloc[i+1]\n            next_high = high_series.iloc[i+1]\n            next_low = low_series.iloc[i+1]\n\n            if sig == -1:\n                # No trade, carry forward capital\n                equity.iloc[i+1] = capital\n                continue\n\n            # Determine entry price with cost\n            if sig == 1:  # long\n                entry = current_price * (1 + entry_cost)\n                # Determine exit price considering stop-loss\n                stop_price = entry * (1 - self.stop_loss_pct) if use_stop else None\n                exit_price = next_close * (1 - exit_cost)\n                if use_stop and next_low <= stop_price:\n                    # Stop triggered: exit at stop price (with exit cost)\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 - exit_cost)\n                ret = (exit_price / entry) - 1\n            else:  # short\n                entry = current_price * (1 - entry_cost)\n                stop_price = entry * (1 + self.stop_loss_pct) if use_stop else None\n                exit_price = next_close * (1 + exit_cost)\n                if use_stop and next_high >= stop_price:\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 + exit_cost)\n                ret = (entry / exit_price) - 1\n\n            # Apply bet size\n            capital *= (1 + ret * self.bet_size)\n\n            self.trades.append({\n                \"entry_time\": signals.index[i],\n                \"exit_time\": signals.index[i+1],\n                \"entry_price\": entry,\n                \"exit_price\": exit_price,\n                \"return\": ret,\n                \"pnl\": capital - self.initial_capital,\n                \"stopped\": use_stop and ((sig == 1 and next_low <= stop_price) or (sig == 0 and next_high >= stop_price))\n            })\n\n            equity.iloc[i+1] = capital\n\n        # Fill any remaining NaNs in equity with last value\n        equity = equity.ffill()\n\n        self.equity_curve = equity\n\n        # Calculate metrics\n        self.metrics = self._compute_metrics()\n\n        return self.metrics\n\n    def _compute_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"Compute metrics from simulation.\"\"\"\n        if not self.trades:\n            return {\n                \"accuracy\": 0.0,\n                \"bets_per_month\": 0.0,\n                \"sharpe\": 0.0,\n                \"max_drawdown\": 0.0,\n                \"total_return\": 0.0,\n                \"n_trades\": 0,\n                \"profit_factor\": 0.0,\n                \"final_equity\": self.initial_capital\n            }\n\n        returns = [t[\"return\"] for t in self.trades]\n        winning = sum(1 for r in returns if r > 0)\n        accuracy = winning / len(returns)\n\n        # Bets per month (entries)\n        n_entries = len(self.trades)\n        if self.equity_curve is not None and len(self.equity_curve) > 0:\n            period_days = len(self.equity_curve) / (24 * 4)  # 15-min candles to days\n        else:\n            period_days = 0\n        months = period_days / 30.44\n        bets_per_month = n_entries / months if months > 0 else 0\n\n        # Sharpe\n        if self.equity_curve is not None:\n            eq_returns = self.equity_curve.pct_change().dropna()\n            if eq_returns.std() > 0:\n                sharpe = (eq_returns.mean() / eq_returns.std()) * np.sqrt(365 * 24 * 4)\n            else:\n                sharpe = 0.0\n\n            # Max drawdown\n            running_max = self.equity_curve.expanding().max()\n            drawdown = (self.equity_curve - running_max) / running_max\n            max_drawdown = abs(drawdown.min())\n        else:\n            sharpe = 0.0\n            max_drawdown = 0.0\n\n        total_return = (self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] - self.initial_capital) / self.initial_capital\n\n        gross_profit = sum(r for r in returns if r > 0)\n        gross_loss = abs(sum(r for r in returns if r < 0))\n        profit_factor = gross_profit / (gross_loss + 1e-10)\n\n        return {\n            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n            \"bets_per_month\": bets_per_month,\n            \"sharpe\": sharpe,\n            \"max_drawdown\": max_drawdown,\n            \"total_return\": total_return,\n            \"n_trades\": len(self.trades),\n            \"profit_factor\": profit_factor,\n            \"final_equity\": self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] if self.equity_curve is not None else self.initial_capital,\n            \"gross_profit\": gross_profit,\n            \"gross_loss\": gross_loss\n        }\n\n    def get_equity_curve(self) -> pd.Series:\n        return self.equity_curve\n\n    def get_trades(self) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        return pd.DataFrame(self.trades)\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":161,"oldLines":15,"newStart":161,"newLines":15,"lines":["         months = period_days / 30.44","         bets_per_month = n_entries / months if months > 0 else 0"," ","-        # Stop triggered: exit at stop price (with exit cost)\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 - exit_cost)\n                ret = (exit_price / entry) - 1\n            else:  # short\n                entry = current_price * (1 - entry_cost)\n                stop_price = entry * (1 + self.stop_loss_pct) if use_stop else None\n                exit_price = next_close * (1 + exit_cost)\n                if use_stop and next_high >= stop_price:\n                    exit_price = stop_price * (1 + exit_cost)\n                ret = (entry / exit_price) - 1\n\n            # Apply bet size\n            capital *= (1 + ret * self.bet_size)\n\n            self.trades.append({\n                \"entry_time\": signals.index[i],\n                \"exit_time\": signals.index[i+1],\n                \"entry_price\": entry,\n                \"exit_price\": exit_price,\n                \"return\": ret,\n                \"pnl\": capital - self.initial_capital,\n                \"stopped\": use_stop and ((sig == 1 and next_low <= stop_price) or (sig == 0 and next_high >= stop_price))\n            })\n\n            equity.iloc[i+1] = capital\n\n        # Fill any remaining NaNs in equity with last value\n        equity = equity.ffill()\n\n        self.equity_curve = equity\n\n        # Calculate metrics\n        self.metrics = self._compute_metrics()\n\n        return self.metrics\n\n    def _compute_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"Compute metrics from simulation.\"\"\"\n        if not self.trades:\n            return {\n                \"accuracy\": 0.0,\n                \"bets_per_month\": 0.0,\n                \"sharpe\": 0.0,\n                \"max_drawdown\": 0.0,\n                \"total_return\": 0.0,\n                \"n_trades\": 0,\n                \"profit_factor\": 0.0,\n                \"final_equity\": self.initial_capital\n            }\n\n        returns = [t[\"return\"] for t in self.trades]\n        winning = sum(1 for r in returns if r > 0)\n        accuracy = winning / len(returns)\n\n        # Bets per month (entries)\n        n_entries = len(self.trades)\n        if self.equity_curve is not None and len(self.equity_curve) > 0:\n            period_days = len(self.equity_curve) / (24 * 4)  # 15-min candles to days\n        else:\n            period_days = 0\n        months = period_days / 30.44\n        bets_per_month = n_entries / months if months > 0 else 0\n\n        # Sharpe on per-trade returns only (avoids inflation from zero-return no-trade periods)\n        if returns and len(returns) > 1:\n            ret_arr = np.array(returns)\n            trades_per_year = (n_entries / max(period_days, 1)) * 365\n            sharpe = (ret_arr.mean() / (ret_arr.std() + 1e-10)) * np.sqrt(trades_per_year)\n        else:\n            sharpe = 0.0\n\n        # Max drawdown\n            running_max = self.equity_curve.expanding().max()\n            drawdown = (self.equity_curve - running_max) / running_max\n            max_drawdown = abs(drawdown.min())\n        else:\n            sharpe = 0.0\n            max_drawdown = 0.0\n\n        total_return = (self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] - self.initial_capital) / self.initial_capital\n\n        gross_profit = sum(r for r in returns if r > 0)\n        gross_loss = abs(sum(r for r in returns if r < 0))\n        profit_factor = gross_profit / (gross_loss + 1e-10)\n\n        return {\n            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n            \"bets_per_month\": bets_per_month,\n            \"sharpe\": sharpe,\n            \"max_drawdown\": max_drawdown,\n            \"total_return\": total_return,\n            \"n_trades\": len(self.trades),\n            \"profit_factor\": profit_factor,\n            \"final_equity\": self.equity_curve.iloc[-1] if self.equity_curve is not None else self.initial_capital,\n            \"gross_profit\": gross_profit,\n            \"gross_loss\": gross_loss\n        }\n\n    def get_equity_curve(self) -> pd.Series:\n        return self.equity_curve\n\n    def get_trades(self) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        return pd.DataFrame(self.trades)\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":170,"oldLines":11,"newStart":170,"newLines":11,"lines":["             sharpe = 0.0"," ","         # Returns metrics dict or None.\"\"\"\n        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n\n        # Train fresh population on this fold's training data\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n            for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n                pop.evolve()\n            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n            print(f\"    Gen {gen+1}: best_train_fitness={best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n\n        # Determine how many non-overlapping folds fit\n        n_folds = 1\n        if total_rows >= 2 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            n_folds = 2\n\n        fold_metrics = []\n        for fold_idx in range(n_folds):\n            # fold_idx=0 (earlier), fold_idx=1 (most recent)\n            valid_end = total_rows - (n_folds - 1 - fold_idx) * val_rows\n            valid_start = valid_end - val_rows\n\n            if valid_start < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                print(f\"Fold {fold_idx+1}: insufficient train samples, skipping.\", flush=True)\n                continue\n\n            valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n            train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:valid_start].copy()\n\n            if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n\n            print(f\"\\nFold {fold_idx+1}/{n_folds}: train={len(train_df)}, valid={len(valid_df)}\", flush=True)\n\n            m = self._run_fold(train_df, valid_df)\n            if m:\n                fold_metrics.append(m)\n\n        if not fold_metrics:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        n = len(fold_metrics)\n        total_trades = sum(m.get('n_trades', 0) for m in fold_metrics)\n\n        if total_trades == 0:\n            combined = fold_metrics[-1].copy()\n            combined[\"n_folds\"] = n\n            return combined\n\n        # Aggregate: weighted accuracy by n_trades, average everything else\n        accuracy = sum(m['accuracy'] * m.get('n_trades', 1) for m in fold_metrics) / total_trades\n        combined = {\n            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n            \"bets_per_month\": sum(m.get('bets_per_month', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"sharpe\": sum(m.get('sharpe', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"profit_factor\": sum(m.get('profit_factor', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"total_return\": sum(m.get('total_return', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n            \"max_drawdown\": max(m.get('max_drawdown', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n            \"n_trades\": total_trades,\n            \"n_folds\": n,\n        }\n\n        print(f\"\\nMulti-fold combined ({n} folds): accuracy={combined['accuracy']:.4f}, \"\n              f\"bets/month={combined['bets_per_month']:.2f}, Sharpe={combined['sharpe']:.3f}, \"\n              f\"total_return={combined['total_return']:.4f}, trades={total_trades}\", flush=True)\n        return combined","originalFile":"\"\"\"\nMain evolution loop for BTC 15-minute directional trading system.\n\nThis module integrates all components and runs the continuous adaptation loop:\n\n1.
